#waitai "Landing Chamber UHV CCG1", <, 6.0e-7
#email "UHVCCG1 pressure below 6.0e-7", "Waiting 1s further", bouet@bnl.gov, sgiorgio@bnl.gov

l1
t2
n

#**********ABOVE THIS LINE IS WHERE TO CHANGE THE GAS CONCENTRATION

setao "PID loop 2 enabled", 1

setao "PID loop 2 reset", 1
t5
setao "PID loop 2 reset", 0
SETDO "GV1 Cryo 1 Gate Valve (Landing Chamber) Main Control (K14)", 0

SETAO "Gate Valve 2 Position", 440

print "Waiting 5 minutes for process gas stabilization"
t300
AC 6000000
DC 6000000
email "Gas stabilized", "restarting growth", bouet@bnl.gov, sgiorgio@bnl.gov
